Chunqiu

Little Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Eight: In a Remote Place, a Light Official Greets a Strong-Willed Mandarin; Outside the Splendid Banquet Hall, There is a Pitiable Wretch

On Cheng Zhiqian's side, he knew very well that Zhang and Li were both incorrigibly vulgar, corrupt officials. However, since they were being so polite and proactively greeting him, he couldn't bring himself to ignore them. Therefore, when Zhang Jiefu approached him with a fawning attitude, he could only force a smile and invite him to sit down. However, Zhang Jiefu had his own agenda. He reached into his coat pocket and rummaged around for a while. He pulled out a small blue cloth bundle, which he unwrapped to reveal a white silk handkerchief package. Opening the handkerchief package, there was a piece of red paper holding two jade objects. One was a finger ring with a semi-circular crack, and the other was a finely carved small jade horse. Cheng Zhiqian was a bit taken aback, wondering if Zhang was also in the jade business and was trying to solicit a sale. Zhang Jiefu, however, smiled ingratiatingly, holding the red paper with both hands. He presented it to Cheng Zhiqian, saying, "This small token is nothing to speak of." Cheng Zhiqian was even more stunned. They had no previous relationship, so why was he offering such valuable gifts? How could he possibly accept them? He repeatedly waved his hands, saying, "I wouldn't dare, I wouldn't dare. I couldn't possibly accept such a generous gift." Zhang Jiefu placed the jade on the table, cupped his hands in a gesture of respect, and said, "I knew Mr. Cheng wouldn't be willing to accept it. But if I explain, Mr. Cheng might reconsider. I have a fellow villager in Xi'an who deals in antiques. I went to see him today, and he casually gave me these two items. He gave them to me not without a purpose. He thinks I know many people in politics and that people might come to Xi'an to buy antiques, so he wants me to introduce them. I think it would be a waste if he just gave these things to me, especially since they're worth about thirty or forty dollars. I really have no use for them. Mr. Cheng is a man of wide connections. As the saying goes, 'A precious sword is given to a hero,' so I'm giving them to Mr. Cheng." (116)

The Physiognomy of Great Men

— (A Rustic Old Man)

After reading Mr. Jiangniao's "Four Strange Physiognomies," which said that famous people in Shanghai all have strange appearances, I was reminded of the physiognomies of the great men of the Party and the Nation. Here's a brief description of a few: (1) The Scholar's Appearance: Mr. Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan of the National Government, is known to all as a pioneer of the revolution and a great statesman of our time. Now in his fifties, he looks like a courteous scholar, no more than forty years old. Like Mr. Hu Hanmin, he is a refined, gentlemanly, fair-skinned scholar. Who would think that he is a great revolutionary? History says that Zhang Zifang had the appearance of a woman, which shows that this is not an exaggeration.

(2) The Bodhisattva's Appearance: Mr. Dai Jitao, the President of the Examination Yuan, used to write essays in the Tianduo Bao and Minquan Bao that were forceful and sharp. I imagined him to be a very different person. Since converting to Buddhism, he has become solemn and compassionate, which overflows from his face. He truly resembles Mr. Wang Yiting, Wang Xiaolai, Di Pingzi, and others in Shanghai, displaying the "Wonderful Appearance of the Tathagata."

(3) The Immortal's Appearance: Mr. Chu Minyi, the Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, is tall and imposing and is skilled in Taijiquan. He resembles one of the Eight Immortals. Perhaps this is because his learning and cultivation have transformed his temperament and appearance.

(4) The Old Woman's Appearance: Mr. Wu Zhihui, a member of the Central Supervisory Committee who calls himself Granny Liu from the Grand View Garden, is getting on in years. His mouth is pursed, and he does have something of an "old woman's appearance." But although Mr. Wu's mouth is pursed, his tongue is like a lotus flower. When he speaks, he is incredibly humorous and profound. He truly deserves to be called Granny Liu.

Snippets

— (Banana Heart)

Xi Shi is a classic example of a beauty in Chinese history. Her hometown is the village of Luoluo in Zhuji, Zhejiang. It is said that a supremely beautiful woman is still born in that village every year, but she is always unlucky and dies young.

Zheng Banqiao said: "We scholars, as soon as we pick up a book, we want to become officials, how to seize money, build big houses, and acquire a lot of land; from the very beginning, we go down the wrong path, and later we get worse and worse, and there is never a good result. "But, how many scholars in the world do not follow this same path?

The Decline of Handicraft Industries

— (Chen Liang)

From the mouths of several fellow villagers who work as craftsmen, I have learned about the recent decline of handicraft industries. Although they are fortunate enough not to have lost their jobs, they are barely making a living, and their lives are extremely difficult. Their short shirts and pants are the color of soy sauce. They don't even have money to get a haircut or take a bath. Now, I will roughly write down what a few of them said below, which is also a serious social problem.

A tailor said, "People all think that clothing is always necessary. Although that's true, it's hard to make money in these times. Ordinary families are tightening their belts on every expense. For example, they turn over old styles, make big clothes smaller, and change the surface of leather clothes. They save on new clothes if they can. As a result, we tailors have no prospects. The worktable is deserted, and the tailors are frowning as they play Wuguan. Do you think things can get better?"

A book cover maker said, "Reading friends all know that nowadays, all books are being changed to hardcover editions. Some time ago, there were still some thread-bound books that used book covers, but now they have also been affected by the competition and dumping of bookstores, which have reprinted many old books and novels as single volumes with foreign paper covers. They consider book covers to be outdated and superfluous. People who make book covers have also been deprived of their livelihoods."

A red sandalwood worker said, "We rely on our strength to make a living. As long as we can pull a saw for a day, we don't have to worry about going hungry. However, everyone these days is pursuing foreign styles and using Western-style furniture. Wealthier people don't even use traditional foreign goods, not to mention everything from flushing toilets to chrome beds. Moreover, small pieces are no longer in the foreign style. Now that we have the strength but no work, is this the end of the line for us?"

There are also grinders, coppersmiths... I can't write about many. In short, some people in the city who have purchasing power admire European culture. Their daily necessities are all imported goods, even the toilet paper they use is not domestic. As for the inland areas, all the clothes and utensils they have must be pawned for money. What purchasing power can they have? The result of the above is that China's national industry is declining, and the handicraft industry is collapsing behind the machine-made industry.

Records of Incense Lingering in the Air

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

This is another very difficult-to-obtain piece of specialized knowledge. After hearing it, we all found it very interesting. Countless gazes were focused on that horse, which had been covered in dust for a long time and had only been hastily cleaned up today, while the Empress Dowager was particularly proud.

Comparing the hard and brave life of people in the past with the life in the imperial palace now, I really don't know how much of a difference there is! It almost makes us unable to believe that the Manchu rulers of the past could have endured such hardships! But some of them are true! Not only the leaders were like this, but all the imperial relatives, ministers, and close attendants in the palace can be said to have been tempered and encouraged in this kind of life every day. At this moment, hundreds of years of luxurious life in China has completely softened us.

By this time, we had visited all three of these not-so-small palaces. We were then led by the Empress Dowager to the open square outside. In the past, almost every day people would rely on their courage and strength to fight for their lives with those wild beasts with sharp claws. Now, it has become a useless wasteland, but the forest on the west side of the square is even more lush and verdant. The tall shadows of the trees flickered on the ground, almost making us suspect that some wild beasts would rush out from inside. The Empress Dowager raised her head and looked around casually, as if sighing with great emotion.

Before we decided to come here, the Empress Dowager had given a brief account of the commemorative history of this day in the Shenyang palace, and had also promised to tell us the details after we saw the forest here. Now, we have arrived in front of the forest, so her promise has been fulfilled! (226)

The Mad Dance of Skeletons

Taste

— Yan Chonglou

Food has various different tastes, and distinguishing these tastes depends entirely on the mouth.

The mouth can taste what is sweet, what is salty, what is sour, what is bitter, and what is spicy.

People's tastes also vary. Generally speaking, most people like to eat sweet things, followed by those who like to eat salty things, then those who like to eat spicy things, and as for those who like to eat bitter things, they are said to be extremely rare.

My second brother loves to eat sour things. Every time he eats noodles, he always complains that the soup is too salty. Once, the family deliberately put only vinegar in his noodle soup. After he finished eating, he asked him how the soup tasted. He said, "The soup tastes very good today, but it's a little less salty." In fact, he didn't know that there was no salt in the soup at all! This is also a joke about taste.

If a cook wants to win the favor of the master, it seems that he must first know the master's taste, but this cannot be regarded as a good cook. A truly good cook is one who can cook delicious dishes that make people adapt to his taste.

Therefore, we ask all cooks to cook standard, compelling delicacies, and at the same time, we hope that all eaters have standard taste-distinguishing tongues.

Places Visited

Night Visit to Tianning Temple

— Huoxueming

The prosperity of Chinese Buddhism has a long history. There are many ancient temples in various places, which have long been famous in the world. Taking Tianning Temple as an example, there are four places. One is outside of Beijing, between Beijing and Zhangjiakou. One is outside of the Tianning Gate in Jiangdu. One is outside of the West Gate of Haikang County in Guangdong. The one I am talking about is that one that was built in the Tang Dynasty outside of the East Gate of Changzhou.

I was traveling to Changzhou, on a cloudy day in early winter without snow. I walked into the train station and saw the city center in the distance, already adorned with bright lights. The night wind was blowing very hard. I hailed a rickshaw and entered the city alone, planning to have a great drink of Lanlu famous wine and devour a lot of thin-skinned, fresh pork, because I was visiting for the first time. I asked the rickshaw puller to take me there. I can say that I was completely ignorant of the names of the streets I passed. However, judging from the city's appearance, where business was not very flourishing in the evening, it was still similar to Gui Cheng in Yixing.

The rickshaw was stopped at Xiaofu Bridge. Fortunately, the lights were burning brightly in the night market. I turned west towards the bridge and caught sight of the Deshun Restaurant on Xianzhi Street. I was very hungry, so I went upstairs to repair my five internal organs. Needless to say, the taste of the wine was not as good as that of Dongpu Xingruanshe in Shaoxing. Li Taibai's "Lanling Wine, Tulip Fragrance" was just an occasional mad rant. On the other hand, Dongpo fatty pork was not inferior to that of Huangzhou in Hubei. I especially loved to eat the sugar-soaked celery, which was beautiful in color, aroma, and taste!

After getting drunk and full, I went downstairs. I thought that my friend who was living in Tianning Temple was sick. Rather than spending money in a noisy inn to spend this lonely cold night, it would be better to go to the ancient temple to talk to him. Moreover, I could also take the opportunity to inquire about his recent health. So I called the temple and asked them not to close the mountain gate too early.

I got back on the rickshaw and looked at the quiet streets and alleys and the changing stars in the moonlight, which was as cool as water. I had some sad feelings of loneliness on the journey. Thanks to the rickshaw puller's arm strength, he pulled me to Dongzhi Street. I listened to the sound of the watchman's gong on the city wall, slowly becoming lighter and farther away.

Turning and lingering, I didn't know how many roads I had traveled. Because of fatigue, I closed my eyes and drew out my thoughts. Although the cold wind easily wakes up a light drunk, I immersed myself in a deeper dream. I even vaguely forgot to look at the buildings in the night.

When the rickshaw came out of the East Gate, in the dim yellow light of the oil lamp, I vaguely recognized three or five starving beggars. They were sitting on the straw, dozing off. So I completed a five-character poem: "Poor drunkards seek refuge, lonely traces occasionally visit Zen. Frosty clothes draped over the midday moon, catkins pressing against the Ding year! Travelers hear hungry birds, mansions boil with pipes and strings. It is our generation's business to lament the times, and there is no way to ask the deaf heaven." I planned to stop for a while and recite it to my sick friend to see how he would criticize it.

Almost at the end of Dongzhi Street, the rickshaw puller suddenly asked, his voice filled with hurried breathing:

"Sir, are you going straight to Tianning Temple?"

This cut off my reverie of savoring the verses.

I opened my eyes and saw a gray crenellated wall on the left, with a curved round doorway in the center. Moonlight was flowing into the square inside the doorway, with tall green trees, sparsely planted, sleeping in clusters. As soon as I pointed to the mountain gate for the rickshaw puller, the rickshaw rolled in sharply.

I don't know if it was because of the sound of the bell on the rickshaw or the accidental night cry of a roosting bird, but it alerted a sleeping yellow dog, which jumped up and barked wildly. In the quiet night, it was really easy to disturb the monks guarding the gate.

At this time, a frozen cloud flew across the sky, temporarily covering the moon. In the empty courtyard, there was only deep darkness, and the leaves were singing in the wind. Coupled with the barking of the dog, the scene was really moving. I saw the mountain gate in front of me. A little red light was vaguely visible, moving as if it were a lighthouse in the dark night. As the light moved closer and closer, I gradually saw the face of the person carrying the lantern. Wasn't that a monk wearing a tall hat? I immediately jumped off the rickshaw, paid the fare, and hurried towards the red light by the tree. I said gratefully:

"Master, you've worked hard! I've made you wait a long time."

"It doesn't matter! Sir, are you coming from the city?" The monk stood still and asked me in return. (To be continued)

Ten Questions and Ten Answers

(1) Doctor Zhao asks: I have been practicing medicine for many years, but I regret that I do not have a perfect medical and nursing textbook to refer to. You have lived in Shanghai for a long time and must have seen and heard a lot. Can you tell me one or two things? Answer: The Guangxie Bookstore at No. 140 Beijing Road, Shanghai (corner of Bote Yuan Road) sells books of the Chinese Medical Association (formerly the Boyihui) and the Chinese Nurses Association. It should have everything you need. You may wish to write for a catalog and read it. (2) Principal Li asks: There are many students in our school, and we plan to implement a new life movement, focusing on hygiene. Where can we purchase hygiene books? Answer: The Shanghai Guangxue Bookstore sells all kinds of hygiene books, forms, models, and lantern slides from the Chinese Hygiene Education Association, the Ministry of Internal Affairs' Health Department, and major bookstores. The styles are complete and it is very convenient to purchase them.

(3) Ms. Huang Lizhu asks: There are more than a dozen infants and young children in my house, who often suffer from diseases, causing both mental and economic losses. Is there any wonderful strategy to remedy this? I hope you can give me some advice! Answer: Infants get sick mostly because parents do not know how to prevent them, and after they get sick, they do not know how to take good care of them. If you have a Parenting Guide (one dollar), Hao Hou Er's Infant and Pediatric Volume (nine yuan), Hao Ci's Pediatric Q&A (two corners), Infant Nursing Method (four corners), or Healthy Living (five yuan) and other books at home, it will be of great help. The above books are sold by Guangxue Bookstore. (4) Colonel Zhang Mingda asks: Mingda has been serving in the Army Hospital for three years. He now plans to study surgery and anatomy. Are there any perfect Chinese texts? Answer: Guangxie Bookstore provides a large number of such medical books. You can write for a catalog.

(5) Mr. Wang Boqin asks: I am burdened with studying at a medical school, and I find it difficult to study and translate medical terms because there are no standard translations. Is there a bookstore in Shanghai that sells standard medical dictionaries? Answer: Dictionaries of standard medical terms approved by the Scientific Terminology Review Committee include the Compilation of Medical Terms, eight yuan; English-Chinese Medical Dictionary, four yuan; Chinese-English Medical Dictionary, two and a half yuan; Chinese Pharmacopoeia, six yuan. All distribution points are at Guangxie Bookstore, No. 140 North Jiujiang Road, Shanghai.

(6) Professor Di Zilin asks: I have long known that the Guangxie Bookstore is the general authority for selling Chinese medical, nursing, and health books. However, I like to read original Yi books. I wonder if there is a bookstore in Shanghai that sells them on consignment? Answer: Oxford University Press and Columbia University Press in New York publish a wealth of medical books. Guangxie Bookstore is the Chinese manager of these two companies; in addition, the bookstore also sells medical books from other major British and American bookstores.

(7) Miss Xue Huifen asks: After class, I like to sing poems and play the piano to entertain myself. I now plan to add more sheet music and songbooks to increase my enjoyment. Please introduce a good edition, I would be grateful! Answer: Sheet music used by famous girls' schools such as Shanghai Chinese and Western Girls' School and St. Mary's are mostly purchased from Guangxie Bookstore; so Miss can also purchase from that bookstore.

(8) Pastor Chen asks: My parishioners are very eager to read various Christian publications in order to understand the truth and preach the gospel, but there are many publishing institutions, and they have repeatedly ordered a book by mail, asking about it back and forth, which takes a lot of time and still results in nothing. Is there a simple and effective way to order by mail? Answer: There are about a hundred Christian publishing institutions, large and small. Shanghai Guangxie Bookstore has spared no expense to collect more than ten thousand kinds of new and old books published by them, and compiled an index (Chinese and English combined one yuan, Chinese version two corners). With this booklet, the title of the book can be established, and you can order from Guangxie Bookstore, which is extremely convenient. (9) Mr. Ge Shangjie asks: I have some experience in studying English. Reading original English versions is ultimately more pure and natural. However, I feel quite inconvenienced to order from abroad every time I return to the country. Is there a bookstore in Shanghai that manages British publications? Answer: Oxford University Press publications are world-renowned, followed by publications from Columbia University Press and more than ten other companies, which Guangxie Bookstore manages on behalf of them; in addition to literature, it also sells specialized scientific books.

(10) Dr. Zhang Chengdao asks: Is the central organization in our country that sells medical, nursing, and health books called Guangxue Bookstore or Guangxie Bookstore? Answer: It was originally called Guangxue Bookstore, but later because the name was easily confused with the Guangxuehui, it was renamed Guangxie Bookstore, and the address is still No. 140 Beijing Road, Shanghai (corner of the Museum Road). Also, the bureau took over the Concord Bookstore.

Education News

Western China Academy Collects Specimens, Yu Jichuan Talks About New Plants Discovered in Xikang

_Rheidium wood and Gung Tung discovered in high mountains_

_Liangshan Yi people loot Han people as slaves_

(Special telegram from Peiping) Yu Jichuan, chairman of the Department of Botany of the Western China Academy, arrived in Peiping today, bringing more than twenty boxes of plant specimens collected in Sichuan. He will borrow the Institute of Quiet Life Biology to test and determine their functions and types. This afternoon, the reporter visited Yu. According to Yu, the Western China Academy was initiated by Lu Zuofu and others and organized in Ba County, Sichuan Province in the 20th year of the Republic of China. Its main work is to investigate, study, test, and improve the production of the west. Currently, there are institutes of biology, physics and chemistry, geology, and agriculture and forestry. The institutes of biology and geology focus on investigation. In addition to private fundraising, the China Cultural Education Fund Committee provides some subsidies. The responsibility I (Yu) assume is the Department of Botany, so I can only tell you about the situation of the Department of Botany. The main task of the Department of Botany is to investigate timber, medicinal materials, oil materials, and other main tasks. Because Sichuan has the most of these kinds of goods, it is divided into early areas. The predetermined purpose of completing the three surveys by 21 years is about (1) Solving the types of plants, (2) The economic value of plant types. Although the scheduled period has expired, there are still some that have not been completed, so supplementary work is still being done. Since Xikang and Sichuan Province are adjacent to each other and lack people to go there for academic and health investigations, people have recently been sent there to collect plant specimens. The province will be divided into four regions, and it is expected to be completed within two years. Zhuanglai may have new discoveries to contribute to the academic community. As for the plants collected in Sichuan Province, more than ten new species have been discovered and announced. The most recently discovered new species include Rheidium wood, Gung Tung, and azaleas (Rhododendron). The first two need to be found on high mountains with a height of two or three thousand meters. What is their function is still being studied. In mid-August and September last year, the Department of Botany sent staff to the large and small deep mountains in southwestern Sichuan to collect specimens. The area is located between ten counties including Leibo, Mabian, Ebian, Pingshan, Xichang, and Huili in Sichuan. It is occupied by the Yi people. They are very harmful to the Han people. Usually, only small merchants go there, so Sichuan people are all secret lairs. Before we went, we received help from the highest local government and gentry in nearby counties, and used Sichuan salt and earth cloth to buy through the responsible protection of the three branches of Mo Yi (ie chieftain) such as Moshimoqu Enxia, so we dared to go. We stayed there for two months and collected many specimens and discovered large forests, about one hundred li long and more than twenty li wide, and drew maps of the deep mountains. However, we encountered difficulties repeatedly. In the middle of the road, we sacrificed our lives, so we could not complete the whole work after all. The people there occupied Zhaojue County in Sichuan Province, and often robbed Han people as slaves, and could buy and sell them at will. Therefore, the Han people who are now there account for eight or nine out of ten of the total population, and they are generally assimilated. If the Chinese people still indulge in the past, the Yi people's harm to Sichuan Province may be even worse than the Communist bandits, (Jin).

The Second Day of the Zhejiang Provincial Social Education Counseling Agency Work Discussion Meeting

The Zhejiang Provincial Social Education Counseling Agency Work Discussion Meeting held by the Zhejiang Education Department continued yesterday (17th) in the auditorium of the Education Department. The attendees gathered at 8:00 am, chaired by Section Chief Jiao of the Third Section of the Department. The meeting was held as usual. First, the chairman reported on the future direction of promoting social education in Zhejiang Province, and then Lin Mu, the principal of the People's Education Experimental School, gave a speech on the past, present, and future of Zhejiang Province's training of talents in people's education, followed by the heads of the social education counseling agencies in the first, second, third, fourth, and fifth provincial school districts reporting on the general situation of the work of their respective agencies. Ministry of Education Compiles Chinese Education Yearbook

Promoting the Truth of Our Country's Education to the International Community

The Ministry of Education approved a letter from the International English Yearbook Society, requesting that a 200,000-word overview of Chinese education be compiled and translated into Western languages for international promotion. The reason is that when international organizations compile education yearbooks for various countries around the world, information on Chinese education is often unclear and lacks a comprehensive and systematic record. Therefore, China will compile a comprehensive and systematic overview of education similar to a national education yearbook and send it to the Society. After receiving the letter, the Ministry of Education has completed the compilation of the characteristics and overview of various levels of education, including higher, secondary, elementary, and social education nationwide. It is currently having members proficient in English translate it separately. The English version will be completed soon and sent to the Society for international promotion.

Ministry of Education Explains the Grade Retention Period for Students Failing the Entrance Examination

The Ministry of Education, in order to explain the grade retention period for students who fail the entrance examination, instructed the Jiangsu Education Department, stating that the grade retention period for secondary school graduation entrance examinations should be handled in accordance with Article 64 of the Secondary School Regulations. (Article 64 stipulates that students who fail three or more subjects in the graduation entrance examination, or who fail only two subjects, but those subjects are any two of the four subjects in junior high school (Chinese, English, Mathematics, Labor), or any two of the five subjects in senior high school (Chinese, English, Mathematics, Physics, Chemistry), should be required to repeat the grade for one year. However, this grade repetition is limited to one time. If they still cannot graduate, a certificate of completion will be issued, and they will be required to withdraw from school.)

Many Schools in Beijing Begin Winter Vacation

Various schools in Nanjing have completed their semester exams on Wednesday of this week. Elementary schools with sixth-grade graduates (such as Fuxi Street Elementary School) held farewell ceremonies for teachers and students on the afternoon of the 17th and started winter vacation, with self-study assignments for the students to take home. Starting from the 18th, all municipal schools will be closed for vacation. Private secondary schools will start their vacations later, with varying schedules. The two provincial experimental elementary schools in Nanjing, established by Jiangsu Province, also started their winter vacation on the 18th. However, due to the customary practices of students from other provinces, the two provincial secondary schools in Nanjing are starting their winter vacation later, as past experience has shown that too few students and too many staff members return if the vacation ends too early. It is said that most secondary schools throughout Jiangsu Province, except for a few, are starting their winter vacation later. Therefore, the two provincial secondary schools in Nanjing are also starting their winter vacation later, around next week.

[P Zhejiang Education Department Issues Production Achievement Competition Regulations>

Production education has been promoted and supervised by the Zhejiang Provincial Education Department in various counties of Zhejiang Province for several years. The production achievements of various localities should be compared to promote observation and improvement. It is learned that the Education Department, in order to facilitate the implementation of this competition in various counties and cities, has specially issued a 14-article outline of the Zhejiang Provincial Production Achievement Competition Regulations for various counties and cities. The competition methods are: (A) exhibitions; (B) production technology demonstrations, with each demonstration focusing on one or two types of products as a principle, and giving priority to demonstrating improvements in local products. Items A and B above may be held simultaneously. The aforementioned outline has been ordered to be followed by the governments of various counties and cities.

Summer Training is Being Prepared, the Ministry of Education Previously

Issued a circular to colleges and universities in this city stating that, except for high school students who should receive centralized training this year and are exempt from summer military training, all colleges and universities should continue to implement summer training according to the original plan. The National Military Training Committee is currently making preparations. All expenses for summer training, such as food, should be borne by the schools.

Centralized Training Will Not Change High School Military Training

Students will definitely participate in centralized training from April 10th to July 10th this year. Rumors of changes are absolutely untrue. The expenses will be borne by the government. All schools should prepare to participate and not adopt a wait-and-see attitude. The students who should receive centralized military training are those who started senior high school in the spring or autumn of the 23rd year of the Republic. Students who start in the spring of this year will receive centralized training next year. The location of the training has been determined by the National Military Training Committee, and the facilities are very complete, but it is still difficult to announce temporarily. According to the reporter's speculation, the Longhua Airport may be more suitable.

Newly Established High Schools Should Receive Military Training

Newly established senior high schools and existing junior high schools that have recently expanded to include senior high school should implement military training from the beginning of the spring semester. All military instructors in each school should be approved by the Military Training Committee. If they are hired privately without approval, it will be investigated and verified. Not only will the military training be invalid, but strict measures will be taken.

All levels of schools in this city, in accordance with the regulations of the Education Bureau's school calendar, started their winter vacation yesterday. Ten Professors Hold First Cultural Construction Symposium Today

Inviting Reporters from Various Newspapers and Professors from Various Universities to Participate

Hoping That This Meeting Will Generate Concrete Proposals

Cai Yuanpei Writes to He Bingsong, Agreeing with the Principles of the Declaration

The ten professors who recently published the "Declaration on Cultural Construction Based on Chinese Values" are holding their first cultural construction symposium at the Zhongshe today at 5:00 PM to discuss various issues related to cultural construction. Those invited to participate include chief editors from various newspapers, university presidents, and over thirty well-known scholars. The minutes will be published in the fifth issue of the "Cultural Construction Monthly." After publication, opinions from various scholars will be solicited again, hoping to generate more concrete opinions so that this movement does not become an impractical one. He Bingsong, who signed the declaration, previously sent the declaration to Cai Yuanpei. Cai Yuanpei has now replied, acknowledging that the principles in the declaration are indestructible and hoping that he can further strive to materialize the two principles of not adhering to old ways and not blindly following others. The original letter is specially reproduced below:

Mr. Bocheng,

I have read the "Declaration on Cultural Construction Based on Chinese Values" you sent. In principle and in abstract theory, it can be said to be indestructible. Confucius said, "When walking with three people, there must be one who can be my teacher. I choose the good and follow it, and change the bad." This is the attitude of not adhering to old ways and not blindly following others. The most important work now is to choose the good. What is good? What is universally recognized as good by mankind, without distinction between Chinese and non-Chinese? What do Chinese people consider good, but non-Chinese people may consider not good? What do non-Chinese people consider good, but Chinese people consider not good? These objects should be listed separately for comparative research. What should be taken and what should be discarded? The components that should be taken should be systematically organized to form a plan for cultural construction. Then, the characteristics of China that still remain can be pointed out. If there is no such plan and one argues in a vacuum, it will inevitably be like Zhang Zhidong's slogan of "Chinese learning for fundamental principles, Western learning for practical application" or Liang Shuming's "Eastern and Western Cultures" - whether you agree or disagree, it's all empty talk. I offer my humble opinion for your reference. With best wishes,

Your younger brother, Cai Yuanpei, January 18th, Year 24 of the Republic

Shen Bao Radio Weekly

The Voltage Withstand Issue of Filtering Capacitors

— (Li Yuanqing)

Recently, I and a friend repaired several different styles of AC radios. Some were purchased ready-made, and some were assembled by ourselves. However, the faults found were exactly the same – all were short circuits in the filter capacitors (Filter Condenser) due to overload. Isn't this a very strange thing?

Commercially available radios, because they strive for compactness and low prices, have to minimize the size and quantity of each component. Therefore, it is only natural that their filter capacitors cannot last. But why do self-made radios also suffer from the same problem? That's a bit puzzling!

I guess that there are probably still many people who do not have a proper understanding of the voltage withstand issue of filter capacitors!

We know that all capacitors have a certain voltage withstand rating (Voltage rating), and exceeding this specified voltage will definitely affect their lifespan. This is an undeniable fact.

The voltage withstand number marked on the capacitor usually represents DC voltage and not AC voltage. If you don't believe it, try connecting a capacitor marked withstanding 500 volts to a 500-volt AC circuit, and you'll likely have a short circuit soon!

To explain the above special phenomenon, we must first talk about the AC voltage itself.

The so-called AC voltage is not as simple as DC voltage. Strictly speaking, if we simply say "AC voltage," it is meaningless. We must specify what kind of AC voltage it is.

Originally, AC voltage itself is a sinusoidal waveform (Sinewave Form). (See attached diagram.) Its value changes at any moment and is not fixed. For the convenience of use, people divide it into the following three values:

(1) Effective AC Voltage The AC voltage changes at any time, as mentioned above. In this way, is it not difficult for us to obtain a definite value? To solve this difficulty, scientists first specified that the value of AC voltage that can produce the same function as DC voltage is called the effective AC voltage (Effective Value of A.C Voltage). The commonly referred to AC voltage or the value measured in an AC voltmeter belongs to this type. Its value is approximately 0.707 times the maximum AC voltage.

(2) Maximum AC Voltage The so-called maximum AC voltage (Maximum Value of A.C Voltage) is the value of AC voltage at its highest peak, so it is also called the peak voltage (Peak Voltage). Its value is approximately 1.41 times the effective value.

(3) Average AC Voltage The average AC voltage mentioned here (Average Value of A.C. Voltage) is not the average value of AC voltage in a cycle (CYc le) (the average value of a cycle is exactly zero), but refers to a half cycle (such as C to D and F to G in the diagram). Its value is approximately 0.9 times the effective value.

The value measured in an AC voltmeter is the effective value, not the maximum value, as mentioned above. In fact, the maximum value can still be encountered twice in each cycle. Therefore, when using capacitors or any other components in an AC circuit, we must be able to withstand the maximum value. In other words, we must be able to withstand at least 1.41 times the effective value to be applicable.

From this perspective, it can be seen that connecting a 500-volt capacitor to an AC circuit actually exposes it to a maximum voltage of 500 * 1.41 = 705 volts! This exceeds its specified voltage withstand rating by nearly half, so how can there be no danger?

For example, the output tube of a certain radio is 45. When the plate voltage is 275 volts and the grid voltage is about 56 volts, and assuming the voltage drop in the low-frequency choke coil is 40 volts, then the effective voltage received by the filter capacitor has reached 371 volts, and its maximum value is 371 x 1.41 = 523.11 volts. Under this condition, if you rashly connect a 500-volt capacitor, it is natural that it will not last.

Sometimes, when the external voltage is too high, or the transformer's waveform is distorted (Wave Dislortion) due to heat, its maximum value often exceeds 1.41 times the effective value. Therefore, for safety reasons, the various insulation materials used in AC circuits are usually based on the standard of being able to withstand 1.5 times the effective value. Therefore, the aforementioned capacitor should use one that can withstand 371 x 1.5 = 556.5 volts. You can choose one that is closest to this number and can withstand 700 volts. (Note: The voltage withstand rating usually marked on the capacitor is an advertising statement from the manufacturer. In fact, it must be discounted by at least 80% to 90%. Therefore, choosing a 700-volt capacitor is not too much.)

Also, heat will affect the voltage withstand number of electrolytic capacitors. Therefore, the position of the capacitor in the radio should be far away from the power transformer and vacuum tubes that generate heat. This point must also be explained in passing.

Converting a Powerful AC Radio to Use Headphones

— Ming Xiang

Since the prevalence of powerful AC radios, headphones seem to have become relics of the past. Those who equipped them earlier now discard them like waste. In fact, under many circumstances, we often feel the need for headphones. For example, when listening to music late at night, using a loudspeaker will inevitably disturb people's sleep, so it is better to switch to headphones for quietness. Comrades who like to play with shortwave, if they use loudspeakers to receive distant radio station music, often get nothing due to the weak signal. If they can switch to headphones, it is not difficult to get unexpected gains. If there are elderly people or those with hearing impairments at home, when others think the volume is adjusted to an appropriate level, they still cannot distinguish it. It is best to connect a headphone separately so that they can also enjoy it.

The following describes two of the simplest methods to make headphones applicable to any radio. The first method is to add a connection to the plate of the final output tube of the radio. A – Connect to the shell diagram Connect to one end of a single-track headphone jack through a blocking capacitor C, and the other end to the radio shell, as shown in Figure 1A. The jack can be installed on the side of the radio wooden box. If the output stage uses two vacuum tubes in a push-pull configuration. The two ends of the jack must each be connected to the plates of the two vacuum tubes through a blocking capacitor, as shown in Figure 1B.

When using, simply insert the headphone plug into the jack to listen. As for the radio's adjustment procedures, it is the same as usual. If it is to receive distant radio stations, only the sound needs to be heard in the headphones. A switch can be added to the voice coil wiring of the loudspeaker to turn it off. If the headphones are added specifically for those with hearing impairments, the switch can be turned on, and the loudspeaker will play at the same time.

The volume adjustment for the first method must be adjusted on the radio's original volume controller. The volume in the headphones cannot be adjusted separately, which is very inconvenient. Therefore, there is the second method to remedy this, that is, the headphones are not directly inserted into the radio's jack, but are replaced with a volume controller, as shown in Figure 2. The ab ends can receive the jack on the radio, and the headphones are inserted into J2. Adjust R to make the volume in the headphones suitable for the individual's needs.

Amplification Frequency Differentiation

— KMK

Whether it is a radio or an amplifier, if you want it to have sufficient volume output, it must have a considerable amplification device. Ordinary amplification is divided into high-frequency amplification (Radio Frepuency Amplifier), intermediate frequency amplification (intermediate Frequency)

Ampjilier) and low-frequency amplification (Audio Frepu ency Amplifier) and other three types. High-frequency amplification is to amplify the high-frequency radio waves emitted by the broadcasting station. After being amplified by the Zhen tube, the output is still high-frequency radio waves. The principle is nothing more than strengthening external radio signals to make the detection stage easier to receive.

Intermediate frequency amplifiers are mostly used in superheterodyne or super-superheterodyne radios. The so-called intermediate frequency has already undergone considerable detection. This item of detection is called the first stage of detection. Although the high-frequency radio waves have been detected, the signals detected by the human ear are still not audible. Therefore, the intermediate frequency is amplified here. And adjust the mutual inductance between the two coils, and then go through the second stage of detection before it becomes the audio low frequency. Because there are many adjustment parts in this item of method, the selectivity is extremely excellent.

Low-frequency amplification is to amplify the audio low-frequency radio waves that have already been detected. The amplification effect of this item is greater than the previous two methods, but because the adjustment parts cannot be increased, the selectivity is of course inferior to the previous method. If multiple stages of low-frequency amplification are added, the tone will inevitably be distorted. Therefore, in imported radios, low-frequency amplification is only used in one stage at most.

The Latest Tone Control Method

— (Li Yuanqing)

The usual method of controlling the tone is probably to connect a fixed capacitor and a variable resistor in parallel in the low-frequency amplification circuit (primary or secondary). When used. Reducing the resistance can cut off (Cut) the higher frequency tones. As a result, the sound emitted by the loudspeaker will be very dull. (Please refer to my previous work "Tone Control Method" in the 16th issue of this journal.)

"Tone Control," as the name suggests. Should be able to control the height of the tone at will. However, the above-mentioned tone controller can only delete the high tones and fully release the low tones. But cannot reduce the bass and maximize the treble. This is its shortcoming!

Western music has a high pitch and many instruments. Whenever twenty or thirty people play together, the sound is loud and there is a lot of noise. Therefore, high-pitched sound waves must be deleted before they can be pleasant to the ear. Chinese music is not like this. For example, a Dan actor sings with a Jinghu. It is usually monotonous. If the above-mentioned tone controller is added, then the listener will think that he is pulling a broken Huqin and drinking a buzzing nose. This is the difference in the organization of Chinese and Western music and the hearing of Chinese and Western people. Do not force them to merge.

Recently, I saw a new type of tone controller in the British Amateur Wireless magazine. But it can remedy the above shortcomings, so I translated it concisely for the same good.

As shown in the figure, L is a choke coil of 3 to 4bv. C is a fixed capacitor of 0.1mf. R is a potentiometer of 10,000 ohms (all connected in parallel in the primary coil of the low-frequency transformer, as shown in the dotted line in the attached figure). When the potentiometer R stops at the center point, this device has little effect. At this time, the tone emitted by the loudspeaker is moderate. When R is rotated to the right, all the higher frequency tones escape from C, and the sound emitted is very dull. When R is rotated to the left, all the lower frequency tones escape from L, and the sound emitted can be very vibrant.

Another Method to Increase Selectivity

— KMK

In Shanghai, where there are many radio stations, the issue of selectivity is indeed difficult to solve. Except for multi-stage high-frequency adjustment and superheterodyne radios with better selectivity, the selectivity of ordinary line radios is particularly bad, and even four or five are mixed together. In addition to shortening the antenna, reducing the primary coil, and adjusting the antenna loop, there seems to be no other way to eliminate the above-mentioned problems. Now the author will introduce an excellent method to increase selectivity, which I think will be welcomed by readers!

The circuit is shown in the figure. L is the primary loop coil, L is the regenerative regenerative coil, L2 is the external adjustment coil, and L3 is the grid loop coil (that is, the secondary loop coil). The selectivity is extremely excellent if designed according to the figure. The coil can be wound on a spider web board with No. 26 silk-covered wire. L must be wound more than ordinary ones. L1 must be determined according to the characteristics of the Zhen tube. L2 and L3 are each wound 65 turns. Arrange the sequences according to the figure, and fix the distance between them after appropriate experimentation. C and C are both 0.00035MF variable capacitors.

Small Experience

Method to Eliminate Vibration Noise of Power Supply Square Panel Iron Sheets

— (Zhou Wenhuan)

The power supply square panel occupies an important position in AC radios (although there are some that do not use it now, they are still a minority). The quality of its work (that is, no heat, no vibration noise, etc.) has a great relationship with the performance of the machine. The author recently repaired a machine for a friend, and his problem is what I am going to tell you about now. The machine was assembled from parts purchased by himself. The circuit is a three-tube powerful AC machine. The power supply square panel is also self-made. The volume and selectivity are not bad. The most annoying thing is that the AC noise is very loud, but after checking its internal parts, all the places where AC noise can be eliminated have been modified. There is no way to do it, so I was asked to repair it. After getting it, I immediately started the inspection and found that the outer edge of the square panel iron core. The iron sheet on the west week has a slight vibration. Pressing it with my hand reduces the AC noise. At that time, I was sure that it must be the thing that was making trouble. How to cure it? The method is very simple: just use white wax liquid (that is, something like a wax candle) and melt it and inject it into the gaps in the iron sheet. Once it cools down, connect the power supply, and the annoying AC noise disappears. If any of the readers have the same problem, please try it too. If you can add three tenths of beeswax to the above-mentioned white wax liquid, it will not immediately lose its effectiveness if the square panel heats up.

New York Stock Market Fluctuated Narrowly

Xinfeng Foreign Company reported yesterday (17th) that the New York stock market was unusually sluggish after President Roosevelt delivered his message, because traders did not know its impact on social legislation and business community. However, the market situation slightly loosened after rising in the early morning, then turned quiet again, and then rose slightly again. The activities were limited to stores and a few special stocks, and the ups and downs of major stocks were extremely narrow. The bond market was firm, but the market atmosphere was dull. Small exchange stocks tended to rise, and Chicago wheat showed an upward trend. The total transaction volume for the day was 740,000 shares. The Dow Jones Index is listed on the left:

Yarn Market Slightly Fell After Rising

The yarn market continued to be firm and gradually showed a stable trend. The rise in US cotton led to a strong bullish sentiment, and the bullish sentiment of Tongji and Tongcheng companies was even stronger, and the market was particularly tight. However, with the deterioration of the surrounding environment and the approaching end of the year, new buyers had little interest, so there was no new development in the market. The golden rooster resisted the short selling and continued to rise. The pre-market opening of standard yarn was firm due to the US cotton report and political news favoring the bulls. The far-term price rose by 25 to 28 pounds, which made the market sentiment even tighter. There were more scattered households resisting short selling. Each month rose by 2.4.5.7 jiao. The opening situation in the afternoon was still high. After shooting to the second and third rounds, it was heard that the spot yarn trading was flat, and the market price of Japanese yarn was low. The closing turned lax again, and the near-term fell by 2.4 jiao. Cotton Resistance to Empty Positions Very Strong

The cotton market is trending well because there is a shortage of deliveries for this month. As of today, the cotton inspection office has reviewed and passed 700 bales of “fire machine” cotton and 1,000 bales of mountain coarse cotton, totaling approximately 1,700 bales. Therefore, those with short positions are not eager to deliver, and engage in active hedging. Simultaneously, the price of US cotton for distant months is rising sharply, further increasing market prices. Indian cotton White Raw Cotton District dark market prices rose sharply by seven rupees.

Insufficient Deliveries This Month

Before the bidding, the market opened weaker, but American cotton, which had been weak, suddenly reversed and rose, with distant months rising even more sharply. Indian cotton coarse goods fell, while fine goods rose. Although receipts for this month are not high, short positions are delivering too little. More than 80,000 bales remain to be settled. Short sellers, seeing insufficient delivery inventory, had to hedge actively, driving up the market. However, large short positions remained unhedged, with each month rising by one or two jiao. After the noon opening, it was heard that the Indian cotton dark market rose another five rupees and twenty-five cents. Market conditions were still good, but until the third closing, some profit-takers closed out positions. This month was unchanged, while distant months fell by five points. Sales were traced to Yuan Da, 1,000 bales; Tong Ji, 1,500 bales; Da Fu, 2,300 bales; Geng Feng, 1,500 bales; Sheng Yuan, 1,200 bales; Yi Kang, 1,000 bales; Shen Ji, 1,300 bales; Yuan Yi, 1,200 bales; Chang Feng, 1,000 bales. U.S. Cotton News Favorable to Bulls

Production Set at 10.05 Million Bales

Yesterday, when the U.S. cotton market opened, dealers and foreign merchants bought in, and prices for each month rose by four to seven points. Subsequently, prices declined as bulls closed out positions. After the Secretary of Agriculture's announcement, market prices rose sharply. However, due to the uncertainty of the gold bar issue and large-scale selling, prices ultimately rose with purchases from local and New Orleans buyers. Some believe that to protect government loans, next year's new cotton will also be subject to new loans and maintenance of handling fees. The closing was firm. Spot prices rose 15 points, nearby contracts rose 12-13 points, and distant months rose 25-28 points. The British cotton market was stable, with spot prices up 5 points and futures up or down 1 point. Indian cotton short accounts were absorbed by hedging and long accounts closed out. Pingguo'er fell by 0.25 rupees, Aomula rose by 3 rupees, and Bairoxi rose by 1 rupee. Original telegram recorded to the left. (17th dispatch)

Furthermore, according to a dispatch from Mumbai, the opening forecast for Bairoxi cotton on the 18th is 247 rupees, an increase of 1 rupee and 25 cents compared to the previous day's closing. Furthermore, according to a dispatch from Washington on the 17th, Secretary of Agriculture Wallace announced today that the cotton production target for 1935, in accordance with the Bankhead Cotton Control Act, is 10.05 million bales (each bale weighing 500 pounds). He also stated that cotton farmers are willing to abandon up to 35 percent of their cotton fields in exchange for subsidies (according to government requirements, cotton farmers must abandon 25 to 30 percent). The carryover for 1935, combined with last year's 700,000 bales (each bale weighing 478 pounds), totals 11.7 million bales. This proves that these bales were not sold in 1934.

Heavy Pressure on Grain Futures Market

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, prices fell across the board. Quotations for imported wheat showed gains of about 1 to 2 jiao in Chicago and about 1 jiao in Canada. When the market opened, the strong prices for imported wheat caused many inside and outside the industry to take a wait-and-see approach. The opening prices for near-term and distant contracts were not much different. However, after the second round of trading, due to the lack of significant shipments from the local "ke bang" for this month and continuous selling pressure from factories for distant contracts, the market turned downward, falling by 2 to 3 fen compared to the opening. At the afternoon opening, the opening price for this month was also unfavorable, once breaking through 4 jiao, falling as low as 3 jiao 9 fen. However, during trading in distant contracts, buying from outside investors and hedging by short sellers caused the market to rebound briefly by 1 to 2 fen. Until the close, trading remained active, with both sides holding their ground, resulting in a balance between supply and demand and prices remaining above the flat line. However, industry insiders generally took a weak outlook due to the continued orders for imported wheat. As a result, the January contract fell by 3 fen and 7.5 li, the February contract fell by 2.5 fen, the March contract fell by 3 fen and 2.5 li, the April contract fell by 2 fen and 7.5 li, the May contract fell by 2.5 fen, and the June contract fell by 1 fen and 7.5 li.

Wheat Initially Firm Then Falls

Yesterday's wheat futures market showed a pattern of initial firmness followed by a decline after the morning opening. Quotations for imported wheat from both Chicago and Canada rebounded by about 1 to 2 jiao. At the opening, the strong prices for imported wheat created a stable market sentiment. However, after the second round of trading, the market sentiment reversed due to the decline in the flour market and the presence of hedged imported wheat in the market. At the afternoon opening, the near-term contracts were especially weak due to the approaching settlement date and the presence of many traders preparing to deliver spot goods. Distant contracts also followed suit with strong selling pressure. Based on the current situation, the low prices for imported wheat may continue to be unfavorable to the bulls. As a result, the January contract fell by 9 fen, the February contract fell by 5 fen, the March contract fell by 6 fen, and the April contract fell by 8 fen. Spot wheat prices also fell by 4 to 5 fen due to a sharp decline in standards and flat demand from factories. Shandong Guide Mingguang wheat was offered at 3 yuan and 8 jiao 4 fen and was reportedly purchased by Fuxin.

The drought and cold in the southwest of Chicago wheat are gradually being discussed by the general public. The market presents a situation where both rises and falls are possible, and neither the bulls nor the bears intend to expand their positions.

Rice Market Stable in the South, Weak in the North

(Shanghai South) Yesterday, more than 40 sources arrived, totaling 7-8,000 shi of goods. Due to the sharp price drop yesterday, the market seemed to have bottomed out. There was some movement in sales, with local sales and buyers from Qingdao continuing to purchase 600-700 packages. Thus, the overall trend turned from stable to tight. Prices for late rice and various thick japonica varieties remained stable except for high-quality goods. Some local goods saw a slight increase. Dujian and Bianyuan, and other varieties, also showed signs of stabilization.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, over 30 ships arrived from various places downstream. Market demand for white japonica short grain was slightly better, while demand for thin rice and Bianyuan was flat, and demand for various superior grains was sluggish. Market prices for high-quality white japonica fell by 1 jiao, and medium and lower grades fell by a small amount (1-2 jiao). Thin rice, Bianyuan, and Yang Dujian also fell slightly. Merchants in the port were reluctant to purchase superior grains, indicating a sluggish market.

Foreign Indica Rice Sales Strong, Prices Rising

Yesterday, the foreign indica rice market saw strong sales of local varieties. Although new shipments of foreign rice continued to arrive, market sentiment remained positive. Foreign rice prices continued to rise in producing regions, and there were even rumors of order registration limits. Local buyers were particularly eager to purchase. Yesterday, 7,000 packages of spot goods and 1,000 tons of futures contracts were sold, primarily to inland areas through local merchants. Prices rose by another 5-6 fen compared to the previous day. Local indica rice prices had initially risen due to shortages and rising prices in producing regions and were expected to be in high demand. However, they were affected by foreign rice and briefly fell. With the rise of foreign rice, demand for local indica rice has increased even further. Yesterday, local merchants sold over 8,000 packages of brown and various indica rices, and inland merchants purchased over 2,000 packages. As a result, the market continued to rise by 5 fen. If demand continues to be strong in the future, prices may have to be increased.

Soybean Shortage, Expecting Price Increase

丨Foreign Firms’ Sesame Reaches the 10 Yuan Mark丨

Yesterday, the soybean market was quite tense because the soybean cake prices went up, and the sources from various regions were not abundant, the inventory was loose day by day, and the grain merchants were determined to hold up the prices, so both buyers and sellers shared a bullish view. Throughout the market, factories and inland merchants purchased more than 30 carloads of Dalian Sipingjie soybeans, more than 2,000 packages of Dalian Xicheng soybeans, one carload of Niuzhuang Bai Mei soybeans, more than 600 packages of Guide soybeans, more than 500 packages of Shashi soybeans, and one carload of Bengbu soybeans and Xin'anzhen soybeans. In addition, the local and inland merchants purchased more than 2,400 packages of Hankou Zha soybeans.

Sesame sales through foreign firms continued to be strong. Yesterday, Sassoon & Co. had a demand for 1,000 tons, but only purchased 600 tons, and the market price reached the 10 yuan mark again, at 10 yuan and 2 cents. Jardine Matheson purchased 200 tons, and the loading price was also 10 yuan and 2 cents. Recorded by Jiang Bang, 100 tons were purchased in the afternoon at a price of only 10 yuan. The sales of spot goods through Dongyang Bang were not weak, so the market remained firm and stable.

Edible Oil Market: Soybean Oil Supply Cannot Meet Demand

丨Soybean Cake Also Continues to Rise丨

Recently, the market conditions for peanut oil and soybean oil have been such that, due to a lack of sources and a daily depletion of inventory, prices have been rising by a few cents per transaction. However, the market was driven up sharply yesterday by a continuous rise in prices reported from Dalian, and the market was eagerly seeking purchases, with merchants only able to supply a small amount to meet demand. As a result, peanut oil rose by 2 jiao, and soybean oil rose by 4 jiao. The overall outlook for the future remains positive and profitable. Since Shantou Bang inquired about futures soybean cake, the soybean cake market has been relatively strong. Yesterday, the current price of Sipai's soybean cake has opened at 1 yuan and 4 jiao and 4 fen.

Nonferrous Metals: Difficulty in Improving Transactions in Pig Lead

Transactions in pig lead have traditionally been most active with yellow litharge factories, paint companies, tin foil factories, and type-setting rooms. Since tea merchants switched to using zinc sheets, the lead boxes they used to make have also decreased in frequency, so its sales are not as lively as before. In recent months, the market has been extremely sluggish due to oversupply, and although the industry has made every effort to find ways and promote sales, the actual transactions are still difficult to improve due to the poor environment. The current market conditions of various merchants are analyzed below:

(Foreign Lead) Recently, frequent shipments have been seen, so the amount accumulated in outside warehouses is very full. However, the local "ke bang" merchants' business has not seen any movement, and the embellishments from local factories are also very few, so the quietness of the market is indescribable. Although the industry has made every effort to promote sales recently, there are no large transactions due to the year-end and tight credit conditions. The market price is estimated at 15 yuan and 2 jiao per dan, with little change compared to the previous period. It is heard that a small amount of trading is taking place at opening prices of 15 yuan and 4 or 5 jiao.

(Domestic Lead) Although the amount of goods arriving is not much, the sales are limited, so the market trend is also very sluggish. The market price is estimated at 14 yuan and 7 or 8 jiao per dan. If sold to retail stores, the opening price is around 15 yuan. Daily transactions are only sporadic, with very few wholesale transactions. It is heard that there are still large quantities of spot goods in Hankou that can be shipped within the month, so the local market sentiment has been very weak recently. It is expected that the market price may tend to soften in the future.
